\subsection{Charge} \label{ComputeCharge}


  		





  229
  229
  
    

  		





  230
  
  
    
This property may be used for economic accounting purposes. It is the charge applied to the users resource usage. 


  		





  231
  
  
    

  		





  232
  
  
    
The attribute \emph{unit} defines the currency used to report the charge, while the attribute \emph{formula} describes the cost computation formula adopted to compute the applied charge.


  		





  
  230
  
    
It is the charge applied to the users resource usage. It has a site dependent meaning and may be used for economic accounting purposes.


  		





  233
  231
  
    

  		





  234
  232
  
    
\begin{itemize}


  		





  235
  
  
    
\item \emph{Charge} MUST be a float.


  		





  236
  
  
    
\item The attribute \emph{unit} MUST be present if \emph{Charge} is specified.


  		





  237
  
  
    
\item The attribute \emph{unit}  MUST be an ISO 4217\footnote{http://www.iso.org/iso/currency\_codes} alphabetic code.


  		





  238
  
  
    
\item The attribute \emph{formula} MUST be present if \emph{Charge} is specified.


  		





  239
  
  
    
\item The attribute \emph{formula} MUST be a string.


  		





  
  233
  
    
\item \emph{Charge} MUST be a decimal.


  		





  240
  234
  
    
\end{itemize}


  		





  241
  235
  
    

  		





  242
  236
  
    
\begin{XMLexample}


  		





  243
  
  
    
<ur:Charge ur:formula="42 units/CPU/day" ur:unit="USD">1.75</ur:Charge>


  		





  
  237
  
    
<ur:Charge>1.75</ur:Charge>


  		





  244
  238
  
    
\end{XMLexample}
